<Rating>4< /Rating><Text>Important to realize:  this is a cafeteria, not a proper restaurant.  Service not so good, staff not friendly, however I love some dishes here.  The ones that come to mind are fried milkfish filet, taro leaves, lentils with a bit of shrimp, squash, several different stews, pork barbecue sausage, adobo (either pork or chicken), and my personal favorite, dinuguan.  Quite a few Americans would be squeamish to try it if they knew the ingredients, but it's a superb comfort food when mixed with rice.  The chef prepares it very well.  I would patronize this place more often if they were to offer the brown rice substitute like so many contemporary eateries do, but perhaps they would rather kill or disable me by complications from diabetes.  If getting the combo, ask for soup.< /Text><Pictures>None< /Pictures>< response>

<Rating>5</Rating>< text>
Was unsure when I arrived, as I normally dont trust empty restaurants- usually means they are not good. This place was a gem in the rough, though. In the middle of nowhere, but nice decor and great food. I feel bad, because I cant imagine a restaurant like this can last with so many empty tables, but they deserve good business. I feel location hurts them, because a place like this in downtown Visalia would be wildly popular. The prices were very reasonable as well. I'm told they are quite busy Friday and Saturday nights, but a place like this should be busy all the time. I hope more people find this place before they cant afford to stay open any longer.</text>

< Review>
We picked up our car at the Los Angeles Airport and drove up to Eureka. We spent the night in Eureka and when we woke up the 2019 GMC Acadia that we were given in LA was having a serious malfunction. When we started the vehicle all the lights on the dash come on and we had multiple error messages pop up on the screen stating "Occupant Restraint Error," "ABS Error" etc. and none of the signals, speedometer, fuel gauge or radio controls would work. We tried to call roadside assistance but was hung up on after explaining our problem to the representative on the phone. So, we checked on our phones and realized there was a Hertz rental location less than a mile away and we decided to drive over.
Upon arriving at the Hertz location in Eureka we felt relieved because there were multiple vehicles (Several Grand Caravans and a couple of Tahoes) on the lot so we figured they would be able to easily switch us into another vehicle. Boy where we wrong! After speaking with the young man at the counter he explained that he did not know what they were going to do because all the vehicles on the lot were reserved for pickups later that day but he thought they had a Chevy Equinox that we could take. After looking at the Equinox we determined that it was much too small for use considering we had 3 adults and a toddler in a chair seat along with all our luggage and also considering that we had reserved a Standard SUV Group L SFAR (Grand Cherokee or Similar) we felt this was a considerable downgrade. We were then told that they could have us ride over to the Eureka Airport location and if they had a vehicle more in the class that we needed. This seemed absurd so we asked if they could look and see what they had or even call over and check for us. We were then told that they had just had a plane land and was busy so they could not call over and ask for us. (Again, this was absolutely absurd and not our problem in the least). While we were still trying to figure it all out a GMC Terrain pulled into the lot to be returned. They ended up giving us the Terrain which we settled for because it was a little bigger than the Equinox. Nevertheless, we were still really cramped in the Terrain while previously we had plenty of room and was extremely satisfied with the Acadia that we originally had. We also were not offered a discounted rate because the vehicle we got stuck with would have actually been cheaper if we had rented that class.
Then to make matters much worse we were told that if they gas was below where it was when we picked it up that we would be charged $9.99 per gallon. I asked how we were supposed to know how much fuel was in the vehicle since the fuel gauge did not work and why they couldn‚Äôt wave that policy due to the circumstance and the agent just shrugged he did not know.
Why could they have not called the location at the airport for us? Why could they not have given us one of the vehicles on the lot that met our needs? Why couldn‚Äôt they have given us a car and gotten one from the airport or another nearby location for the pickup later in the day? We were already extremely inconvenienced by the situation and they were not trying to help us. We are repeat customers that had already paid for our rental and it actually seemed that they were trying to be as difficult as possible.
After this experience I think we are going to cancel our Gold Membership and start using Enterprise again because we did not have these kind of issues.< /Review>

< Text>
I'm a Hertz Gold Member and reserved my car online. When I went to pick it up, I was not given any explanation of charges, verbally or even a printed out receipt. I was unknowingly given a more expensive car than I had reserved, and charged $25 extra per day for it, again, not told to me when I picked up the car. When the car was returned, the guy at the desk, Jake, basically said there was nothing he could do about it, and to call Hertz if we wanted to. I called the Billing dept at Hertz and got yelled at by  the lady I spoke to, who told me to "take responsibility for this." I stayed courteous throughout the whole call because I really want to give her the benefit of the doubt that she's not a mean person; I really hope Hertz records their phone conversations. She then gave me the number for the Hertz location where I picked up the car and told me to talk to the manager, and when I called, it turns out that particular manager hasn't worked for Hertz for years. I had to call for three consecutive days, leaving a message & callback number every time (no one ever called me back), until a manager finally picked up the phone. The manager, Jessie, said she believed Jake when he said he gave me a verbal explanation of charges, even though she did confirm with him that I was never presented with a paper printout of the charges when I picked up the keys. She decided not to believe me, and I got the feeling that even if she did believe me, she wouldn't have done anything about it.</Text>

Never again.</review>

< text>
Since 1977, Eggie's has been serving Sacramento. I feel honored to be served here! I walked in at felt at ease, as though I was walking in to a familiar place, shattering my perceptions of space and time.

Biscuits and gravy were spot on delicious! Garlic in the gravy adds a yum delight. Homemade biscuits. This is one of the best plates of B&G I've had in my travels. And my blood is white country sausage gravy. My soul yearns daily for B&G.

Bacon was crispy salty good. Coffee was standard yet decent.

Wait staff was super per friendly. This place has a home nostalgic feel. I enjoyed my brief time here and wanted to linger to hear secrets told by the walls.

T-shirts available for purchase.

This restaurant is amazing. Sit at the counter if you want. You'll be glad you did.<//text>

<userid>112570901091282062838< /userid><Name>Nicole Luebker< /Name><Date>1527972330322< /Date>< Rating>
3</Rating>
< review>
I'll get into why I gave this place 3 stars in a minute, but first I wanna say the service here was excellent. Very attentive and friendly staff.
When it comes to the food, it was OK. My boyfriend ordered an omelet with hash browns. I ordered blueberry pancakes with eggs. I enjoyed my bf's meal much more than my own. The omelet was delicious, and if I ever go back that is what I will order. My pancakes were a little gummy and my eggs were flavorless. All they would have to do is add salt and pepper and I'm sure my eggs would have been much better.
Lastly, the worst part of my experience was the atmosphere on the inside. From the outside, Eggies looks like a cute little retro diner. But on the inside, man can it use some renovation! The side of the restaurant in which we were seated was dark, gloomy, and the carpet was dirty. The booths look like they were about to fall apart. The chairs are miss matched. Nothing exciting on the walls. Dull colors. It was just sad inside. If they were to make a few changes with the decor it would make all the difference.<//review>
